@057A *, ,BU ZUNG 'JUG PHYAG RGYA CHEN PO THOB BYED DU MTSUNGS

GNYIS GANG RUNG DU LHUNG BAR 'GYUR TE, PHAL CHER PHYOGS LHUNG GI
MUN PAS BSGRIBS NAS RGYU MTSAN YANG DAG PA BRJOD PA'I LAG 'THOGS
TE, 'DI NI BDAG GI LTO ZA SA'I LUGS YIN NO ZER BA TSUN GYIS RANG
PHYOGS MA GTOGS RGYAL BA'I BKA' DANG MTHUN PA'I THOG MA'I LUGS

BZANG GZHAN THAMS CAD SANGS RGYAS THOB BYED KYI PHYOGS SU YANG

SKYON GYIS BDAG NI GRUB

MTHA' SU LA YANG PHYOGS RIS MED PAS THAMS CAD LA DAG SNANG CAN

SKYES PA NA SBYOR LAM DROD THOB CING, TING 'DZIN DE NI STONG
NYID LA DMIGS PA'I ZHI LHAG ZUNG 'BREL GYI RNAL 'BYOR YANG YIN
NO, ,DE NAS DROD SOGS BZHI RIM GYIS BRGYUD DE CHOS NYID MNGON
SUM DU MTHONG BAR 'GYUR RO, ,DE

BYED PA'I BAR CHAD MED LAM DANG, MTHONG SPANG LAS DNGOS SU GROL
BA'I RNAM GROL LAM GNYIS LTA BU YANG, STONG NYID LA GNYIS SNANG
NUB PA'I MNYAM GZHAG YE SHES GCIG GI RGYUN YIN NA YANG, RANG GI
SEMS KYI CHOS NYID

@145A *, ,MTHONG SPANG DANG BRAL BA'I BRAL CHA MNGON SUM DU MA
RTOGS PA DANG, RTOGS PA LA SOGS PA'I CHOS NYID LA GNYIS SNANG
NUB TSUL PHRA RAG GI KHYAD PAR CHEN PO YOD, DE LAS LANGS PA'I SA
DANG PO'I RJES THOB TU YON TAN BRGYA PHRAG BCU GNYIS MNGON DU
BYED CING,

DE BZHIN DU SGOM LAM SA BCU LA YANG, MNYAM GZHAG TU SGRIB PRAL
CHOS SKU LHAG PAR MTHONG TSUL MI 'DRA BA DANG, RJES THOB TU DES
DRANGS PA'I GZHAN DON 'PHRIN LAS KYI YON TAN GONG DU 'PHAL BA'I
RIM PA BSAM GYIS MI KHYAB PA YOD PA RED, 'DI DAG BSHAD SHES PA'I
DRUNG NAS NYAN SHES

PAS DA LTA NAS NYAN NA, YON TAN CHUNG NGUS RLOM PA'I NGA RGYAL
ZHI BA DANG, YON TAN DE RNAMS LA THOB 'DOD SKYE BA DANG, YON TAN
CAN DE RNAMS LA SKYABS SU 'GRO BA DANG, RANG GZHAN SA LAM MTHO
DMAN GYI RGYUD TSOD ZIN PA SOGS DGOS PA CHEN PO YOD DO, ,GSUM PA
BRTZAMS PA

MTHAR PHYIN PA'I DGE BA BSNGO BA NI, DE SKAD SMRA BA MANG THOS
SPONG BA PA, ,BLO BZANG CHES KYI RGYAL MTSAN ZHES BYA STE, ,DGE
BAS 'GRO KUN ZHI SGO GNYIS PA DANG, ,BRAL BA'I LAM 'DIS MYUR DU
RGYAL GYUR CIG ,CES GSUNGS, DE YANG GONG DU DAM BCAS PA LTAR
TSIG DON DE SKAD RDZOGS

PAR SMRA BA PO RANG NYID LUNG RTOGS KYI BSTAN PA YONGS RDZOGS
KYI BDAG PO MTSAN 'DI ZHES BYA BAR ZHAL GYIS BZHES NAS, BRTZAMS
PA MTHAR PHYIN PA'I DGE BAS 'GRO KUN ZHI BDE THAR PA LA 'JUG
PA'I SGO MI 'DRA BA GNYIS SU MED PA'I GCIG PU DE KHO NA NYID JI
BZHIN RTOGS

PA'I LAM 'DI THOB NAS, THABS KHYAD PAR CAN GYI GROGS DANG MA

SANGS RGYAS THOB PAR GYUR CIG CES BSNGO BAR MDZAD DO, ,MDOR NA
ZHI SGO GCIG TU GSUNGS PA 'DI 'DRA BA LA DES PA PHUL DU BYUNG BA
GNYIS DRANG RGYU

YOD PA LAM RIM CHEN MOR GSUNGS PA LTAR NGES PAR MDZAD DGOS, DE
